The following features are not yet available in stable releases.\\n59: \\n60: - The experimental \\\"deferred actions\\\" feature, enabled by passing the `-allow-deferral` option to `terraform plan`, permits `count` and `for_each` arguments in `module`, `resource`, and `data` blocks to have unknown values and allows providers to react more flexibly to unknown values.\\n61: - `terraform test cleanup`: The experimental `test cleanup` command. In experimental builds of Terraform, a manifest file and state files for each failed cleanup operation during test operations are saved within the `.terraform` local directory. The `test cleanup` command will attempt to clean up the local state files left behind automatically, without requiring manual intervention.\\n62: - `terraform test`: `backend` blocks and `skip_cleanup` attributes:\\n63:   - Test authors can now specify `backend` blocks within `run` blocks in Terraform Test files. Run blocks with `backend` blocks will load state from the specified backend instead of starting from empty state on every execution. This allows test authors to keep long-running test infrastructure alive between test operations, saving time during regular test operations.\\n64:   - Test authors can now specify `skip_cleanup` attributes within test files and within run blocks. The `skip_cleanup` attribute tells `terraform test` not to clean up state files produced by run blocks with this attribute set to true. The state files for affected run blocks will be written to disk within the `.terraform` directory, where they can then be cleaned up manually using the also experimental `terraform test cleanup` command.\\n65: \\n66: ## Previous Releases\\n67: \\n68: For information on prior major and minor releases, refer to their changelogs:\\n69: \\n70: - The previous behavior, which treated any non-empty value as `true`, is no longer supported. To migrate: Update any scripts or automation that set these environment variables to explicitly use `\"true\"` or `\"false\"` instead of other values. ([#37601](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37601))\n\n### New Features\n\n- **command/validate**: The `validate` command now validates the backend configuration block. It checks that the specified backend type exists, all required attributes are present, and that the backend's own validation logic passes. This catches backend configuration errors earlier in the development cycle. ([#38021](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38021))\n\n- **variables/outputs**: You can now set a `deprecated` attribute on variable and output blocks to indicate they are deprecated. When a deprecated variable receives a value or a deprecated output is referenced, Terraform will emit a deprecation warning. This enables graceful deprecation of module inputs and outputs. ([#38001](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38001))\n\n- **backend/s3**: S3 backend now supports AWS credential authentication via `terraform login`. Users can now authenticate to AWS using the standard `terraform login` command, which leverages AWS credential sources configured through the CLI credentials system. ([#37967](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37967))\n\n- **core/builds**: Terraform now produces official binary builds for Windows ARM64 (Windows on ARM64 architecture). This enables Terraform to run natively on ARM64-based Windows systems. ([#32719](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/32719))\n\n### Enhancements\n\n- **command/init**: The init command now skips dependencies declared in development overrides. This allows you to use `terraform init` with developer overrides while installing dependencies not declared in the override file, improving the development workflow. ([#37884](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37884))\n\n- **command/init**: Log timestamps in `terraform init` now include millisecond precision, providing better granularity for debugging and monitoring init operations. ([#37818](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37818))\n\n- **provisioners/ssh**: SSH-based provisioners (file and remote-exec) now have re-enabled support for PowerShell on Windows targets. This restores the ability to use PowerShell scripting within remote-exec and file provisioner commands. ([#37794](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37794))\n\n- **testing/test-framework**: The Terraform Test framework now allows the use of functions within mock blocks. This enables more sophisticated mocking strategies in test files. ([#34672](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/34672))\n\n- **terraform-core**: Improved detection of deprecated resource attributes and blocks. The analysis now more accurately identifies deprecated configurations and provides clearer guidance on replacements. ([#38077](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38077))\n\n### Bug Fixes\n\n- **cloud/network**: Terraform Cloud and registry discovery network requests are now more resilient. Temporary network errors and service-related issues are handled with improved retry logic, reducing transient failure rates. ([#38064](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38064))\n\n- **command/apply**: Fixed a bug where a plan file intended for one workspace could be applied against a different workspace. Terraform now raises an explicit error if the plan's workspace doesn't match the current workspace. ([#37954](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37954))\n\n- **command/state**: The `state show` command now explicitly fails with exit code 1 when it fails to render the named resources' state. Previously, it could exit with code 0 despite failing to display the state. ([#37933](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37933))\n\n- **command/init-json**: Fixed `terraform init -json` to properly format all backend configuration messages as JSON instead of mixing JSON with plain text output. This ensures consistent JSON output for scripting and automation. ([#37911](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37911))\n\n- **command/show-json**: Fixed a crash in `terraform show -json` when the plan contains ephemeral resources with preconditions or postconditions. The JSON serialization now properly handles these resource configurations. ([#37834](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37834))\n\n- **command/plan**: Fixed an issue where a refresh-only plan with no changes could incorrectly return a non-zero exit code. The command now correctly returns exit code 0 when there are no changes to display. ([#37406](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37406))\n\n- **lifecycle**: The `replace_triggered_by` attribute now reports a clear error when given an invalid attribute reference that doesn't exist in the target resource. Previously, this could cause confusing behavior or silent failures. ([#36740](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/36740))\n\n- **backend/init**: Fixed a nil pointer dereference crash that could occur during `terraform init` when the destination backend returns an error. Terraform now handles backend errors more gracefully. ([#38027](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38027))\n\n- **stacks/plan**: Fixed stacks to send progress events when a plan fails. This ensures proper UI integration and status reporting when stack planning encounters errors. ([#38039](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38039))\n\n- **stacks/component-instances**: Component instances now properly report no-op plans and applies. This fixes a UI inconsistency with convergence destroy plans in stack operations. ([#38049](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/38049))\n\n- **testing/junit-output**: File-level error diagnostics are now included in JUnit XML skipped test elements. This ensures that CI/CD pipelines can detect validation failures from test execution. ([#37801](https://github.com/hashicorp/terraform/issues/37801))\n\n### Deprecations\n\nNone in this release.\n\n### Performance Improvements\n\nNone in this release.\n\n---\n\n## Experimental Features\n\nExperiments are only enabled in alpha releases of Terraform CLI. The following features are not yet available in stable releases.\n\n- **Deferred Actions**: The experimental \"deferred actions\" feature, enabled by passing the `-allow-deferral` option to `terraform plan`, permits `count` and `for_each` arguments in `module`, `resource`, and `data` blocks to have unknown values. This allows providers to react more flexibly to unknown values during planning.\n\n- **Test Cleanup**: The experimental `terraform test cleanup` command helps manage state files left behind by failed test cleanup operations. In experimental builds, manifest files and state files are saved within the `.terraform` directory, and this command attempts to clean them up automatically.\n\n- **Test Backend Blocks**: Test authors can now specify `backend` blocks within `run` blocks in Terraform Test files. Run blocks with backend blocks load state from the specified backend instead of starting from empty state, allowing test infrastructure to persist between test operations.\n\n- **Test Skip Cleanup**: Test authors can now use the `skip_cleanup` attribute in test files and within run blocks. This preserves state files produced by marked run blocks in the `.terraform` directory for manual cleanup or inspection.\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":12320,"cache_read_input_tokens":57831,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":12320},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"b7b91044-abb3-4b6e-a689-5392fe6f323a","uuid":"dfcede2f-37e8-4ef4-9ad7-94374b139d01"}
